  1951. # [15:46] <ejpbruel> baku: i have a platform patch that introduces a second global to each worker, which is lazily loaded when we initialize the debugger
  1952. # [15:46] <ejpbruel> baku: the debugger runs on that second global and inspects the first one
  1953. # [15:46] <baku> ejpbruel, ok
  1954. # [15:46] <ejpbruel> baku: at some point when the main script hit a breakpoint, we need to create the illusion that the main thread is paused
  1955. # [15:46] <kats> and yet i can curl that file just fine
  1956. # [15:46] <kats> weird
  1957. # [15:46] * Quits: mconley (mconley@moz-FBB7D102.cable.teksavvy.com) (Input/output error)
  1958. # [15:47] <ejpbruel> on the main thread, we do so by supressing event handling on the debuggee's window
  1959. # [15:47] * Quits: ekr (Adium@moz-FAC44BDF.hfc.comcastbusiness.net) (Quit: Leaving.)
  1960. # [15:47] <ejpbruel> and then entering a nested event loop
  1961. # [15:47] * Joins: mconley (mconley@moz-FBB7D102.cable.teksavvy.com)
  1962. # [15:47] <ejpbruel> that way we can still talk to the debugger but things like timeouts wont fire on the main thread
  1963. # [15:47] <baku> ejpbruel, ok
  1964. # [15:47] * Quits: rbarnes (rbarnes@BA2E35F6.5E7AC5F4.FAA4474F.IP) (Input/output error)
  1965. # [15:47] <ejpbruel> on the worker thread however, both the debugger and the debuggee use the same event queue
  1966. # [15:47] <ejpbruel> there is no notion of nested queues there
  1967. # [15:48] <ejpbruel> so instead i introduced a second event queue for debugger runnables
  1968. # [15:48] <baku> correct.
  1969. # [15:48] <ejpbruel> and rewrote the workers event loop so that it drains both queues
  1970. # [15:48] <ejpbruel> however, if the debugger spins up a nested event loop
  1971. # [15:48] <ejpbruel> we only drain the debugger queue
  1972. # [15:48] <ejpbruel> this effectively blocks timeouts etc
  1973. # [15:48] <ejpbruel> while still allowing communication with the main thread
  1974. # [15:49] <ejpbruel> since debugger messages are sent over that second queue
  1975. # [15:49] * Quits: mconley (mconley@moz-FBB7D102.cable.teksavvy.com) (Ping timeout)
